<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>suspended, pendant, pendulous, <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> suspension

***подвести.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подвести.html>подвести́</a> (2708)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвести.html>подвести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podvestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подводить.html>подводи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bring closer
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвести.html>подвести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часы́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvestí</b> časý</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to alter the watch/clock; to set the watch/clock</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвести.html>подвести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:войско.html>войска́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:граница.html>грани́це</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvestí</b> vojská k graníce</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bring troops to the border</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:живот.html>живо́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голод.html>го́лода</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвести.html>подвело́</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U nevó živót ot góloda <b>podveló</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He is awfully hungry; he feels pinched.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to place <i>(under)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвести.html>подвести́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:фундамент.html>фунда́мент</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">podvestí fundáment</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to underpin</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвести.html>подвести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыша.html>кры́шу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvestí</b> dom pod krýšu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to roof the house</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвести.html>подвести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мина.html>ми́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvestí</b> mínu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to mine, to torpedo</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to substantiate <i>(with)</i>, to support <i>(with)</i>, to account <i>(for by)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвести.html>подвести́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:итог.html>ито́ги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">podvestí itógi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to sum up</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвести.html>подвести́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:баланс.html>бала́нс</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">podvestí baláns</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to balance the accounts</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвести.html>подвести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:база.html>ба́зу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvestí</b> bázu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to provide a basis/reasoning; to prove</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвести.html>подвести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:теория.html>тео́рию</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наблюдаемый.html>наблюда́емые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:факт.html>фа́кты</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvestí</b> teóriju pod nabljudájemyje fákty</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">suggest a theory to explain the observable facts</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to class, to group together, to present <i>(as)</i>, to depict <i>(as)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвести.html>подвести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уголовный.html>уголо́вную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:статья.html>статью</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvestí</b> délo pod ugolóvnuju statʹju</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">present the affair as a criminal offence</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to drive <i>(at)</i>, to suggest
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>К</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пытаться.html>пыта́етесь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвести.html>подвести́</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">K čemú vy pytájetesʹ <b>podvestí</b>?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">What are you driving at/trying to prove?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to let down, to do a bad turn</li>
<li>to pencil, to outline
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвести.html>подвести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бровь.html>брови</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvestí</b> brovi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pencil one's eyebrows</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***подвиг.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подвиг.html>по́двиг</a> (2938)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвиг.html>по́двиг</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pódvig</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвиг.html>по́двига</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвиг.html>по́двиги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвиг.html>по́двигов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>exploit, feat, heroic deed
<ul><li><dl><dd><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white">Р. <li>(heroic) deed, labor
<ul><li><dl><dd><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>С</a>. Л. <li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:известный.html>Изве́стно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> глуповец <a href = vnd.unilang:иметь.html>име́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совесть.html>совесть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:покладистый.html>покла́дистую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:готовый.html>готов</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:всякое.html>вся́кий</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвиг.html>по́двиг</a></span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:лишь.html>лишь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:инициатива.html>инициати́ва</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвиг.html>по́двига</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:исходить.html>исходи́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лица</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:могущий.html>могу́щего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:водка.html>во́дку</a>. </span></li>

***подвигаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подвигаться.html>подвига́ться</a> (17127)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвигать.html>подвига́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podvigátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвигаться.html>подвига́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podvigátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвинуться.html>подви́нуться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to move
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвигаться.html>подвига́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:назад.html>наза́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvigatʹsja</b> nazád</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to move/draw back</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвигаться.html>подвига́ться</a></b> бли́же</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvigatʹsja</b> blíže</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to move/come/draw nearer</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to advance, to progress</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to advance <i>(in one's career)</i></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвигать.html>подвига́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podvigátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвигать.html>подви́гать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podvígatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвигающийся.html>подвига́ющийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podvigájuščijsja</span>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвижник.html>подви́жник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podvížnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвижник.html>подви́жника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвижник.html>подви́жники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвижник.html>подви́жников</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">подвиза́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podvizátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвизаться.html>подвиза́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podvizátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rush (somewhere), to move forward</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to strive</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to labor, to act, to work <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">expressing oneself in some area of activity</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to distinguish oneself in military matters, to fight bravely</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">подвиза́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podvizátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подвинуться.html>подви́нуться</a> (13385)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвинуть.html>подви́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podvínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвинуться.html>подви́нуться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podvínutʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвигаться.html>подвига́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to move
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвинуться.html>подви́нуться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:назад.html>наза́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvínutʹsja</b> nazád</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to move/draw back</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвинуться.html>подви́нуться</a></b> бли́же</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvínutʹsja</b> blíže</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to move/come/draw nearer</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to advance, to progress</li></ol>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвинуть.html>подви́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podvínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***подвод.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подвода.html>подво́д</a> (23209)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подводить.html>подводи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podvodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвода.html>подво́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podvód</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвода.html>подво́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвода.html>подво́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвод.html>подво́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>supply, delivery</li>
<li>admission, intake</li></ol>

***подводить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подводить.html>подводи́ть</a> (6289)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водить.html>води́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подводить.html>подводи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podvodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подвести.html>подвести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bring closer
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подводить.html>подводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часы́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvodítʹ</b> časý</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to alter the watch/clock; to set the watch/clock</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подводить.html>подводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:войско.html>войска́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:граница.html>грани́це</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvodítʹ</b> vojská k graníce</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bring troops to the border</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:живот.html>живо́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голод.html>го́лода</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подвести.html>подвело́</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U nevó živót ot góloda <b>podveló</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He is awfully hungry; he feels pinched.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to place <i>(under)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подводить.html>подводи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:фундамент.html>фундаме́нт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">podvodítʹ fundamént</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to underpin</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подводить.html>подводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыша.html>кры́шу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvodítʹ</b> dom pod krýšu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to roof the house</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подводить.html>подводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мина.html>ми́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvodítʹ</b> mínu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to mine, to torpedo, to cause somebody a lot of trouble/to set someone up</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to substantiate <i>(with)</i>, to support <i>(with)</i>, to account <i>(for by)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подводить.html>подводи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:итог.html>ито́ги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">podvodítʹ itógi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to sum up</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подводить.html>подводи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:баланс.html>бала́нс</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">podvodítʹ baláns</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to balance the accounts</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подводить.html>подводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:база.html>ба́зу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvodítʹ</b> bázu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to provide a basis/reasoning; to prove</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подводить.html>подводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:теория.html>тео́рию</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наблюдаемый.html>наблюда́емые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:факт.html>фа́кты</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvodítʹ</b> teóriju pod nabljudájemyje fákty</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">suggest a theory to explain the observable facts</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to class, to group together, to present <i>(as)</i>, to depict <i>(as)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подводить.html>подводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уголовный.html>уголо́вную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:статья.html>статью́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvodítʹ</b> délo pod ugolóvnuju statʹjú</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">present the affair as a criminal offence</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to drive <i>(at)</i>, to suggest</li>
<li>to let down, to do a bad turn</li>
<li>to pencil, to outline
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подводить.html>подводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бровь.html>бро́ви</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podvodítʹ</b> bróvi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pencil one's eyebrows</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ворот.html>воро́та</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voróta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ня</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подворотня.html>подворо́тня</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podvorótnja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подворотня.html>подворо́тни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подворотня.html>подворо́тни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подворотня.html>подворо́тен</a></b>)
